# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs

type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []
    |

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []
    | hd::

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []
    | hd::tl => if idx ==

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []
    | hd::tl => if idx == 0

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []
    | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then tl

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []
    | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then tl else hd :: remove

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []
    | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then tl else hd :: remove(idx

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []
    | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then tl else hd :: remove(idx -

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []
    | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then tl else hd :: remove(idx - 1,

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []
    | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then tl else hd :: remove(idx - 1, tl

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Remove a todo item by its index #
let remove: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
  fun idx, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []
    | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then tl else hd :: remove(idx - 1, tl) end in
